# Neovim

[![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rockerBOO/awesome-neovim?style=flat)](https://github.com/rockerBOO/awesome-neovim/stargazers)

# Awesome Neovim [![Awesome](https://awesome.re/badge-flat.svg)](https://awesome.re)

<a href="https://neovim.io/"><img src="https://neovim.io/logos/neovim-mark-flat.png" align="right" width="144"/></a>

> A collection of awesome Neovim plugins. Mostly targeting Neovim specific features.
> This means Vim-compatible plugins are not listed here.

[Neovim](https://neovim.io/) is a Vim-based text editor engineered for extensibility and usability, to encourage new applications and contributions.
It has some [builtin plugins](https://neovim.io/doc/user/plugins.html#plugins) as well as a rich API for many more to be developed.

## Plugin Manager

- [alyxshang/nuwa.nvim](https://source.alyxshang.boo/alyxshang/nuwa.nvim) - A light package manager.
- [lewis6991/pckr.nvim](https://github.com/lewis6991/pckr.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lewis6991/pckr.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/lewis6991/pckr.nvim/stargazers) - Spiritual successor of `wbthomason/packer.nvim`.
- [savq/paq-nvim](https://github.com/savq/paq-nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/savq/paq-nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/savq/paq-nvim/stargazers) - Package manager written in Lua.
<!--lint disable double-link -->
- [NTBBloodbath/cheovim](https://github.com/NTBBloodbath/cheovim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NTBBloodbath/cheovim?style=flat)](https://github.com/NTBBloodbath/cheovim/stargazers) - A configuration switcher written in Lua. Inspired by [chemacs](https://github.com/plexus/chemacs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/plexus/chemacs?style=flat)](https://github.com/plexus/chemacs/stargazers).
<!--lint enable double-link -->
- [folke/lazy.nvim](https://github.com/folke/lazy.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/folke/lazy.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/folke/lazy.nvim/stargazers) - A modern plugin manager, featuring a graphical interface, async execution, a lockfile and more.
  - [cosmicbuffalo/super_lazy.nvim](https://github.com/cosmicbuffalo/super_lazy.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cosmicbuffalo/super_lazy.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/cosmicbuffalo/super_lazy.nvim/stargazers) - An extension to `folke`'s `lazy.nvim`, enables use of multiple lockfiles for large teams that want to combine your shared/personal configurations.
- [alex-popov-tech/store.nvim](https://github.com/alex-popov-tech/store.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alex-popov-tech/store.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/alex-popov-tech/store.nvim/stargazers) - Plugins discovery tool with hourly updated database, and one-key installation for `lazy.nvim` and `vim.pack`.
- [lumen-oss/rocks.nvim](https://github.com/lumen-oss/rocks.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lumen-oss/rocks.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/lumen-oss/rocks.nvim/stargazers) - A modern approach to plugin management using LuaRocks, inspired by Cargo.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.deps](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-deps.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-deps.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-deps.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` for managing other plugins. Uses Git and built-in packages to install, update, clean, and snapshot plugins.
- [wsdjeg/nvim-plug](https://github.com/wsdjeg/nvim-plug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wsdjeg/nvim-plug?style=flat)](https://github.com/wsdjeg/nvim-plug/stargazers) - Asynchronous plugin manager written in Lua.
- [piersolenski/plugin-addict.nvim](https://github.com/piersolenski/plugin-addict.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/piersolenski/plugin-addict.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/piersolenski/plugin-addict.nvim/stargazers) - A stupidly simple way to quickly install plugins.
- [OriginCoderPulse/synapse.nvim](https://github.com/OriginCoderPulse/synapse.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OriginCoderPulse/synapse.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/OriginCoderPulse/synapse.nvim/stargazers) - A modern, lightweight plugin manager with beautiful UI, intelligent dependency management, tag/branch support, and post-install command execution.
- [zuqini/zpack.nvim](https://github.com/zuqini/zpack.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zuqini/zpack.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/zuqini/zpack.nvim/stargazers) - A thin layer on top of `vim.pack` to support lazy-loading and `lazy.nvim`'s declarative spec.
<!--lint disable double-link -->
[**⬆ back to top**](#contents)
<!--lint enable double-link -->

## LSP

**(requires Neovim 0.5)**

- [romus204/referencer.nvim](https://github.com/romus204/referencer.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romus204/referencer.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/romus204/referencer.nvim/stargazers) - Lightweight, asynchronous that uses the LSP to show references to functions, methods, types and other.
- [Dan7h3x/signup.nvim](https://github.com/Dan7h3x/signup.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Dan7h3x/signup.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Dan7h3x/signup.nvim/stargazers) - a little smart `lsp_signature` helper with awesome features.
<!--lint disable awesome-spell-check-->
- [neovim/nvim-lspconfig](https://github.com/neovim/nvim-lspconfig) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neovim/nvim-lspconfig?style=flat)](https://github.com/neovim/nvim-lspconfig/stargazers) - Quickstart configurations for the LSP client.
<!--lint enable awesome-spell-check-->
- [nvim-lua/lsp-status.nvim](https://github.com/nvim-lua/lsp-status.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-lua/lsp-status.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-lua/lsp-status.nvim/stargazers) - This is a plugin/library for generating statusline components from the built-in LSP client.
- [nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim](https://github.com/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvimdev/lspsaga.nvim/stargazers) - A light-weight LSP plugin based on the built-in LSP with a highly performant UI.
- [kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb](https://github.com/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb?style=flat)](https://github.com/kosayoda/nvim-lightbulb/stargazers) - The plugin shows a lightbulb in the sign column whenever a `textDocument/codeAction` is available at the current cursor position.
- [onsails/lspkind.nvim](https://github.com/onsails/lspkind.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onsails/lspkind.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/onsails/lspkind.nvim/stargazers) - The plugin adds VSCode-like icons to LSP completions.
- [ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy](https://github.com/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy?style=flat)](https://github.com/ojroques/nvim-lspfuzzy/stargazers) - A small plugin to make the LSP client use FZF.
- [gfanto/fzf-lsp.nvim](https://github.com/gfanto/fzf-lsp.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gfanto/fzf-lsp.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/gfanto/fzf-lsp.nvim/stargazers) - Enable the power of FZF fuzzy search for the built-in LSP.
- [ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim](https://github.com/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/ray-x/lsp_signature.nvim/stargazers) - LSP signature hint when you type.
- [smjonas/inc-rename.nvim](https://github.com/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/smjonas/inc-rename.nvim/stargazers) - Provides an incremental LSP rename command based on the command-preview feature.
- [rmagatti/goto-preview](https://github.com/rmagatti/goto-preview) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rmagatti/goto-preview?style=flat)](https://github.com/rmagatti/goto-preview/stargazers) - Previewing native LSP's goto definition calls in floating windows.
- [jubnzv/virtual-types.nvim](https://github.com/jubnzv/virtual-types.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jubnzv/virtual-types.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/jubnzv/virtual-types.nvim/stargazers) - Show type annotations as virtual text.
- [marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim](https://github.com/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/marilari88/twoslash-queries.nvim/stargazers) - Provide inline virtual text displaying TypeScript types for the inspected variables.
- [retran/meow.yarn.nvim](https://github.com/retran/meow.yarn.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/retran/meow.yarn.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/retran/meow.yarn.nvim/stargazers) - Interactive LSP type and call hierarchy explorer with a tree view, live preview, navigation breadcrumbs, and a custom node renderer.
- [ray-x/navigator.lua](https://github.com/ray-x/navigator.lua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ray-x/navigator.lua?style=flat)](https://github.com/ray-x/navigator.lua/stargazers) - Learn existing code quickly and navigate code like a breeze. A swiss army knife makes exploring LSP and Tree-sitter symbols a piece of cake.
- [hedyhli/outline.nvim](https://github.com/hedyhli/outline.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hedyhli/outline.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/hedyhli/outline.nvim/stargazers) - A significantly enhanced and refactored fork of `symbols-outline.nvim`.
- [stevearc/aerial.nvim](https://github.com/stevearc/aerial.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stevearc/aerial.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/stevearc/aerial.nvim/stargazers) - A code outline window for skimming and quick navigation.
- [hasansujon786/nvim-navbuddy](https://github.com/hasansujon786/nvim-navbuddy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hasansujon786/nvim-navbuddy?style=flat)](https://github.com/hasansujon786/nvim-navbuddy/stargazers) - A simple popup display that provides breadcrumbs like navigation feature but in keyboard centric manner, inspired by the `ranger` file manager.
- [tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim](https://github.com/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/tamago324/nlsp-settings.nvim/stargazers) - Setup LSP with JSON or YAML files.
- [jakewvincent/texmagic.nvim](https://github.com/jakewvincent/texmagic.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jakewvincent/texmagic.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/jakewvincent/texmagic.nvim/stargazers) - Enhance the lspconfig settings for Texlab by defining any number of custom LaTeX build engines and selecting them with magic comments.
- [aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim](https://github.com/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/aznhe21/actions-preview.nvim/stargazers) - Fully customizable previewer for LSP code actions.
- [mfussenegger/nvim-lint](https://github.com/mfussenegger/nvim-lint) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mfussenegger/nvim-lint?style=flat)](https://github.com/mfussenegger/nvim-lint/stargazers) - An asynchronous linter plugin, complementary to the built-in Language Server Protocol support.
- [b0o/SchemaStore.nvim](https://github.com/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/b0o/SchemaStore.nvim/stargazers) - Provide access to the [SchemaStore](https://github.com/SchemaStore/schemastore) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SchemaStore/schemastore?style=flat)](https://github.com/SchemaStore/schemastore/stargazers) catalog.
- [j-hui/fidget.nvim](https://github.com/j-hui/fidget.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/j-hui/fidget.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/j-hui/fidget.nvim/stargazers) - Standalone UI for LSP progress.
<!--lint disable double-link-->
- [scalameta/nvim-metals](https://github.com/scalameta/nvim-metals) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/scalameta/nvim-metals?style=flat)](https://github.com/scalameta/nvim-metals/stargazers) - Provides a better experience while using [Metals](https://scalameta.org/metals/), the Scala Language Server, using the built-in LSP support.
<!--lint enable double-link-->
- [junnplus/lsp-setup.nvim](https://github.com/junnplus/lsp-setup.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/junnplus/lsp-setup.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/junnplus/lsp-setup.nvim/stargazers) - A simple wrapper for `nvim-lspconfig` and `mason-lspconfig` to easily setup LSP servers.
- [amrbashir/nvim-docs-view](https://github.com/amrbashir/nvim-docs-view) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/amrbashir/nvim-docs-view?style=flat)](https://github.com/amrbashir/nvim-docs-view/stargazers) - Display LSP hover documentation in a side panel.
- [mfussenegger/nvim-jdtls](https://github.com/mfussenegger/nvim-jdtls) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mfussenegger/nvim-jdtls?style=flat)](https://github.com/mfussenegger/nvim-jdtls/stargazers) - Extensions for the built-in LSP support for the Eclipse JDT Language Server.
- [Kasama/nvim-custom-diagnostic-highlight](https://github.com/Kasama/nvim-custom-diagnostic-highlight) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Kasama/nvim-custom-diagnostic-highlight?style=flat)](https://github.com/Kasama/nvim-custom-diagnostic-highlight/stargazers) - Inline diagnostics popup-highlight much like `coc-nvim` but based on `vim.diagnostic`.
- [mrcjkb/haskell-tools.nvim](https://github.com/mrcjkb/haskell-tools.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrcjkb/haskell-tools.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mrcjkb/haskell-tools.nvim/stargazers) - Seamless integration for Haskell development tools like `haskell-language-server` and Hoogle.
- [~chinmay/clangd_extensions.nvim](https://sr.ht/~chinmay/clangd_extensions.nvim) - Off-spec `clangd` features for the built-in LSP client.
- [ranjithshegde/ccls.nvim](https://github.com/ranjithshegde/ccls.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ranjithshegde/ccls.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/ranjithshegde/ccls.nvim/stargazers) - Use off-spec extensions of ccls LSP and browse AST.
- [idanarye/nvim-buffls](https://github.com/idanarye/nvim-buffls) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/idanarye/nvim-buffls?style=flat)](https://github.com/idanarye/nvim-buffls/stargazers) - Add LSP functionality to specific buffers.
- [error311/wayfinder.nvim](https://github.com/error311/wayfinder.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/error311/wayfinder.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/error311/wayfinder.nvim/stargazers) - Guided code exploration from the current symbol with a keepable trail.
- [DNLHC/glance.nvim](https://github.com/DNLHC/glance.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DNLHC/glance.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/DNLHC/glance.nvim/stargazers) - A pretty window for previewing, navigating and editing your LSP locations.
- [linrongbin16/lsp-progress.nvim](https://github.com/linrongbin16/lsp-progress.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/linrongbin16/lsp-progress.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/linrongbin16/lsp-progress.nvim/stargazers) - A performant LSP progress status.
- [jinzhongjia/LspUI.nvim](https://github.com/jinzhongjia/LspUI.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jinzhongjia/LspUI.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/jinzhongjia/LspUI.nvim/stargazers) - A modern and useful UI that wraps LSP operations.
- [VidocqH/lsp-lens.nvim](https://github.com/VidocqH/lsp-lens.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VidocqH/lsp-lens.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/VidocqH/lsp-lens.nvim/stargazers) - Display function references above function definition like IDEA codelens.
- [Wansmer/symbol-usage.nvim](https://github.com/Wansmer/symbol-usage.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Wansmer/symbol-usage.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Wansmer/symbol-usage.nvim/stargazers) - Display references, definitions and implementations of document symbols.
- [creativenull/efmls-configs-nvim](https://github.com/creativenull/efmls-configs-nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/creativenull/efmls-configs-nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/creativenull/efmls-configs-nvim/stargazers) - An unofficial collection of linters and formatters configured for efm-langserver to work with built-in LSP.
- [creativenull/diagnosticls-configs-nvim](https://github.com/creativenull/diagnosticls-configs-nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/creativenull/diagnosticls-configs-nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/creativenull/diagnosticls-configs-nvim/stargazers) - An unofficial collection of linters and formatters configured for diagnostic-languageserver to work with built-in LSP.
- [hinell/lsp-timeout.nvim](https://github.com/hinell/lsp-timeout.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hinell/lsp-timeout.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/hinell/lsp-timeout.nvim/stargazers) - Automatically start/stop idle/unused LSP servers; keeps RAM usage low.
- [nvimtools/none-ls.nvim](https://github.com/nvimtools/none-ls.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvimtools/none-ls.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvimtools/none-ls.nvim/stargazers) - A reloaded `null-ls.nvim` to use your editor as a language server to inject LSP diagnostics, code actions, and more via Lua.
- [Zeioth/none-ls-autoload.nvim](https://github.com/Zeioth/none-ls-autoload.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Zeioth/none-ls-autoload.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Zeioth/none-ls-autoload.nvim/stargazers) - Auto-load/unload `none-ls` sources installed with `mason`, with support for built-in and external sources.
- [vxpm/ferris.nvim](https://github.com/vxpm/ferris.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vxpm/ferris.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/vxpm/ferris.nvim/stargazers) - Interact with Rust-Analyzer's LSP extensions.
- [mrcjkb/rustaceanvim](https://github.com/mrcjkb/rustaceanvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrcjkb/rustaceanvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mrcjkb/rustaceanvim/stargazers) - A heavily modified fork of rust-tools.nvim that does not require a `setup` call and does not depend on nvim-lspconfig.
- [soulis-1256/eagle.nvim](https://github.com/soulis-1256/eagle.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/soulis-1256/eagle.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/soulis-1256/eagle.nvim/stargazers) - Mouse-hover LSP hints.
- [stevanmilic/nvim-lspimport](https://github.com/stevanmilic/nvim-lspimport) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stevanmilic/nvim-lspimport?style=flat)](https://github.com/stevanmilic/nvim-lspimport/stargazers) - Automatically resolves imports for undefined terms. Useful with `pyright` language server.
- [jmbuhr/otter.nvim](https://github.com/jmbuhr/otter.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jmbuhr/otter.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/jmbuhr/otter.nvim/stargazers) - Provides LSP features and a nvim-cmp completion source for languages embedded in other documents.

Display one line diagnostic messages where the cursor is, with icons and colors.

## Syntax

- [nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter](https://github.com/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter/stargazers) - Tree-sitter configurations and abstraction layer.
- [romus204/tree-sitter-manager.nvim](https://github.com/romus204/tree-sitter-manager.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romus204/tree-sitter-manager.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/romus204/tree-sitter-manager.nvim/stargazers) - A lightweight Tree-sitter parser manager to replace the archived `nvim-treesitter` plugin.
- [nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter-textobjects](https://github.com/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter-textobjects) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter-textobjects?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter-textobjects/stargazers) - Create your own textobjects using Tree-sitter queries.
- [RRethy/nvim-treesitter-textsubjects](https://github.com/RRethy/nvim-treesitter-textsubjects) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RRethy/nvim-treesitter-textsubjects?style=flat)](https://github.com/RRethy/nvim-treesitter-textsubjects/stargazers) - Location and syntax aware text objects which _do what you mean_.
- [kylechui/nvim-surround](https://github.com/kylechui/nvim-surround) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kylechui/nvim-surround?style=flat)](https://github.com/kylechui/nvim-surround/stargazers) - A plugin for adding/changing/deleting surrounding delimiter pairs.

Supports dot-repeat, different search methods, "last"/"next" extended mappings, Tree-sitter integration, and more.

## Fuzzy Finder

- [nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim](https://github.com/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim/stargazers) - Telescope.nvim is a highly [extendable](https://github.com/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim/wiki/Extensions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim/wiki/Extensions?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-telescope/telescope.nvim/wiki/Extensions/stargazers) A highly extensible fuzzy finder over lists.
- [vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf](https://github.com/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf?style=flat)](https://github.com/vijaymarupudi/nvim-fzf/stargazers) - A Lua API for using FZF. Allows for full asynchronicity for UI speed and usability.
- [camspiers/snap](https://github.com/camspiers/snap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/camspiers/snap?style=flat)](https://github.com/camspiers/snap/stargazers) - An extensible fuzzy finder. Similar to Telescope, and optimized for performance, especially when grepping in large codebases.
- [ibhagwan/fzf-lua](https://github.com/ibhagwan/fzf-lua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ibhagwan/fzf-lua?style=flat)](https://github.com/ibhagwan/fzf-lua/stargazers) - The Lua version of `fzf.vim`, high-performance and fully async, supports `nvim-web-devicons`, Git indicators, LSP, quickfix/location lists and more. Also supports [`skim`](https://github.com/lotabout/skim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lotabout/skim?style=flat)](https://github.com/lotabout/skim/stargazers) as its fzf binary.
- [willyelm/pulse.nvim](https://github.com/willyelm/pulse.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/willyelm/pulse.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/willyelm/pulse.nvim/stargazers) - A single entrypoint for commands. Use prefixes to quickly access diagnostics, Git and more via pickers.
- [jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide](https://github.com/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide?style=flat)](https://github.com/jvgrootveld/telescope-zoxide/stargazers) - Telescope integration for [zoxide](https://github.com/ajeetdsouza/zoxide) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ajeetdsouza/zoxide?style=flat)](https://github.com/ajeetdsouza/zoxide/stargazers), a smart directory picker that tracks your usage.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.fuzzy](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-fuzzy.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-fuzzy.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-fuzzy.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` with functions to perform fuzzy matching of one string to others along with fast Telescope sorter.
- [axkirillov/easypick.nvim](https://github.com/axkirillov/easypick.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/axkirillov/easypick.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/axkirillov/easypick.nvim/stargazers) - Easypick lets you easily create Telescope pickers from arbitrary console commands.

- [zachyarbrough/anchor.nvim](https://github.com/zachyarbrough/anchor.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zachyarbrough/anchor.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/zachyarbrough/anchor.nvim/stargazers) - Pin project-specific directories for instant fuzzy searching. Inspired by Harpoon.

## Buffers

- [TheLazyCat00/workspaces-nvim](https://github.com/TheLazyCat00/workspaces-nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TheLazyCat00/workspaces-nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/TheLazyCat00/workspaces-nvim/stargazers) - Pin files to specific keys within a project workspace, giving you quick access to your most important files.
- [dzfrias/arena.nvim](https://github.com/dzfrias/arena.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dzfrias/arena.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/dzfrias/arena.nvim/stargazers) - A smart (frecency-based) buffer switcher.
- [backdround/tabscope.nvim](https://github.com/backdround/tabscope.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/backdround/tabscope.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/backdround/tabscope.nvim/stargazers) - Make tab-local buffers.
- [akasataikisiti/tabLocalBuffer.nvim](https://github.com/akasataikisiti/tabLocalBuffer.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/akasataikisiti/tabLocalBuffer.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/akasataikisiti/tabLocalBuffer.nvim/stargazers) - Keeps a per-tab buffer list and provides its own bnext / bprevious style navigation that cycles only within the current tab.
- [j-morano/buffer_manager.nvim](https://github.com/j-morano/buffer_manager.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/j-morano/buffer_manager.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/j-morano/buffer_manager.nvim/stargazers) - Add one or more buffers, reorder them, save them inside a file or just delete them very easily from a small floating window.
- [kazhala/close-buffers.nvim](https://github.com/kazhala/close-buffers.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kazhala/close-buffers.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/kazhala/close-buffers.nvim/stargazers) - Delete multiple Vim buffers based on different conditions.

- [axkirillov/hbac.nvim](https://github.com/axkirillov/hbac.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/axkirillov/hbac.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/axkirillov/hbac.nvim/stargazers) - Automatically close buffers you are not working on.
- [ChuufMaster/buffer-vacuum](https://github.com/ChuufMaster/buffer-vacuum) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChuufMaster/buffer-vacuum?style=flat)](https://github.com/ChuufMaster/buffer-vacuum/stargazers) - Set a maximum number of buffers to keep open and intelligently delete the oldest buffers over the maximum.
- [mong8se/buffish.nvim](https://github.com/mong8se/buffish.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mong8se/buffish.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mong8se/buffish.nvim/stargazers) - A buffer switcher in the spirit of dirvish or vinegar.

## Colorscheme

Each colorscheme will have one or more of the tags listed below. If a tag is missing
then it is not supported:

<!--lint disable awesome-list-item-->
- **_`[TS]`_** - Has Tree-sitter highlighting.
- **_`[LSP]`_** - Has LSP Semantic Tokens support.
- **_`[L/D]`_** - Has both "light" and "dark" variants.
- **_`[Lua]`_** - Is written in Lua.
- **_`[Fnl]`_** - Is written in Fennel.
<!--lint enable awesome-list-item-->

- [ThorstenRhau/token](https://github.com/ThorstenRhau/token) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ThorstenRhau/token?style=flat)](https://github.com/ThorstenRhau/token/stargazers) - **_`[TS][LSP][L/D][Lua]`_** Token has warm tones and careful contrast, with full Tree-sitter and LSP integration.
- [oskarnurm/koda.nvim](https://github.com/oskarnurm/koda.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oskarnurm/koda.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/oskarnurm/koda.nvim/stargazers) - **_`[TS][LSP][L/D][Lua]`_** Code's quiet companion. A minimalist colorscheme, written in Lua.
- [yonatan-perel/lake-dweller.nvim](https://github.com/yonatan-perel/lake-dweller.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yonatan-perel/lake-dweller.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/yonatan-perel/lake-dweller.nvim/stargazers) - **_`[TS][LSP][Lua]`_** Dark and opinionated with selective highlighting aiming to be readable at a glance.
- [silentium-theme/silentium.nvim](https://github.com/silentium-theme/silentium.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/silentium-theme/silentium.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/silentium-theme/silentium.nvim/stargazers) - **_`[TS][Luа]`_** Pragmatic and monochrome theme with the goal to increase reading speed and reduce eye strain by highlighting only what is needed.
- [serhez/teide.nvim](https://github.com/serhez/teide.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/serhez/teide.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/serhez/teide.nvim/stargazers) - **_`[TS][LSP][L/D][Lua]`_** A fork of folke's `tokyonight.nvim` with a different color palette.
- [kuri-sun/yoda.nvim](https://github.com/kuri-sun/yoda.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kuri-sun/yoda.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/kuri-sun/yoda.nvim/stargazers) - **_`[TS][L/D][Lua]`_** Muted green palette for focused, balanced editing.

Not quite dark, not quite light — just right.

- [sontungexpt/witch](https://github.com/sontungexpt/witch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sontungexpt/witch?style=flat)](https://github.com/sontungexpt/witch/stargazers) - **_`[TS][LSP][L/D][Lua]`_** The primary stinvim distro colorscheme includes the default feature of dimming inactive windows, along with various other customization options for users.

### Colorscheme Creation

- [tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim](https://github.com/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/tjdevries/colorbuddy.nvim/stargazers) - A colorscheme helper. Written in Lua! Quick and Easy Color Schemes.
- [norcalli/nvim-base16.lua](https://github.com/norcalli/nvim-base16.lua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/norcalli/nvim-base16.lua?style=flat)](https://github.com/norcalli/nvim-base16.lua/stargazers) - Programmatic Lua library for setting base16 themes.
- [rktjmp/lush.nvim](https://github.com/rktjmp/lush.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rktjmp/lush.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/rktjmp/lush.nvim/stargazers) - Define colorschemes as a DSL in Lua, with real-time feedback.
- [Iron-E/nvim-highlite](https://github.com/Iron-E/nvim-highlite) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Iron-E/nvim-highlite?style=flat)](https://github.com/Iron-E/nvim-highlite/stargazers) - A colorscheme generator that is "lite" on logic for the developer.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.base16](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-base16.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-base16.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-base16.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` with fast implementation of base16 theme for manually supplied palette.
- [ThemerCorp/themer.lua](https://github.com/ThemerCorp/themer.lua) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ThemerCorp/themer.lua?style=flat)](https://github.com/ThemerCorp/themer.lua/stargazers) - A simple highlighter with a huge collection of colorschemes. It also has ability to create colorschemes for your editor and other supported apps (such as `kitty` and `alacritty`).
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.colors](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-colors.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-colors.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-colors.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` to tweak and save any color scheme. Also can animate transition and convert between some color spaces.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.hues](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-hues.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-hues.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-hues.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` to generate configurable color scheme. Takes only background and foreground colors as required arguments. Can adjust number of hues for non-base colors, saturation, accent color, plugin integration.
- [loganswartz/polychrome.nvim](https://github.com/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/loganswartz/polychrome.nvim/stargazers) - A colorscheme micro-framework, with support for specifying colors directly in many different formats (sRGB, HSL, Oklab, XYZ and more, with intelligent chroma clipping), live editing preview, and a simple DSL.
- [svermeulen/text-to-colorscheme](https://github.com/svermeulen/text-to-colorscheme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/svermeulen/text-to-colorscheme?style=flat)](https://github.com/svermeulen/text-to-colorscheme/stargazers) - Allows the user to generate colorschemes with a text prompt using OpenAI's GPT API.
- [RRethy/base16-nvim](https://github.com/RRethy/base16-nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RRethy/base16-nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/RRethy/base16-nvim/stargazers) - A base16 colorscheme builder. Includes support for Tree-sitter and LSP highlight groups.

### Colorscheme Switchers

- [DrKJeff16/which-colorscheme.nvim](https://github.com/DrKJeff16/which-colorscheme.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DrKJeff16/which-colorscheme.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/DrKJeff16/which-colorscheme.nvim/stargazers) - Cycle between colorschemes using either custom or autogenerated `which-key.nvim` bindings.
- [itsfernn/auto-gnome-theme.nvim](https://github.com/itsfernn/auto-gnome-theme.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/itsfernn/auto-gnome-theme.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/itsfernn/auto-gnome-theme.nvim/stargazers) - Fast colorscheme switcher following GNOME system's light/dark mode (based on `gsetting monitor`).
- [flashcodes-themayankjha/fkthemes.nvim](https://github.com/flashcodes-themayankjha/fkthemes.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flashcodes-themayankjha/fkthemes.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/flashcodes-themayankjha/fkthemes.nvim/stargazers) - A fast, lightweight and powerful theme switcher written in Lua.
- [4e554c4c/darkman.nvim](https://github.com/4e554c4c/darkman.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/4e554c4c/darkman.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/4e554c4c/darkman.nvim/stargazers) - Follow the system dark-mode setting on Linux.
- [f-person/auto-dark-mode.nvim](https://github.com/f-person/auto-dark-mode.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/f-person/auto-dark-mode.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/f-person/auto-dark-mode.nvim/stargazers) - Follow the system appearance on macOS.
- [zaldih/themery.nvim](https://github.com/zaldih/themery.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zaldih/themery.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/zaldih/themery.nvim/stargazers) - A new way to change the colorscheme on the fly like in VSCode.
- [linrongbin16/colorbox.nvim](https://github.com/linrongbin16/colorbox.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/linrongbin16/colorbox.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/linrongbin16/colorbox.nvim/stargazers) - Load all the ultra colorschemes into your editor's player.
- [CWood-sdf/pineapple](https://github.com/CWood-sdf/pineapple) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CWood-sdf/pineapple?style=flat)](https://github.com/CWood-sdf/pineapple/stargazers) - Install any colorscheme in your config without leaving your terminal. Collects every colorscheme on the internet and allows you to preview them all before installing.
- [BrunoCiccarino/gardenal](https://github.com/BrunoCiccarino/gardenal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BrunoCiccarino/gardenal?style=flat)](https://github.com/BrunoCiccarino/gardenal/stargazers) - Gardenal is a theme switcher, which allows the user to create keyboard shortcuts to switch between themes with one click.
- [LmanTW/themify.nvim](https://github.com/LmanTW/themify.nvim/tree/main) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LmanTW/themify.nvim/tree/main?style=flat)](https://github.com/LmanTW/themify.nvim/tree/main/stargazers) - A lightweight colorscheme manager and switcher inspired by Themery.nvim and Lazy.nvim.
- [nishu-murmu/ThemeSwitch.nvim](https://github.com/nishu-murmu/ThemeSwitch.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nishu-murmu/ThemeSwitch.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nishu-murmu/ThemeSwitch.nvim/stargazers) - Light weight color scheme switcher.

## Motion

- [HawkinsT/pathfinder.nvim](https://github.com/HawkinsT/pathfinder.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HawkinsT/pathfinder.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/HawkinsT/pathfinder.nvim/stargazers) - Enhances gf/gF/gx with look-ahead and smarter file, line/column number, and link resolution. Also provides visual targets for files/links, new motion commands, and link description retrieval.
- [nolleh/warp.nvim](https://github.com/nolleh/warp.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nolleh/warp.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nolleh/warp.nvim/stargazers) - Jump based on labels to file paths, URLs, and Markdown links from any buffer.

## Keybinding

- [RutaTang/compter.nvim](https://github.com/RutaTang/compter.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RutaTang/compter.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/RutaTang/compter.nvim/stargazers) - Power and extend the ability of `<C-a>` and `<C-x>` with customized patterns.

- [chrisgrieser/nvim-recorder](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/nvim-recorder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisgrieser/nvim-recorder?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/nvim-recorder/stargazers) - Simplifying and improving how you interact with macros.
- [sontungexpt/bim.nvim](https://github.com/sontungexpt/bim.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sontungexpt/bim.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/sontungexpt/bim.nvim/stargazers) - Enhances insert mode key mapping by showing typed keys in real time, without waiting for timeoutlen. It provides a responsive and intuitive insert-mode experience, ideal for complex input workflows like ime.
- [folke/which-key.nvim](https://github.com/folke/which-key.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/folke/which-key.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/folke/which-key.nvim/stargazers) - Shows a popup with possible keybindings of the command you started typing.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.clue](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-clue.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-clue.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-clue.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` to show next key clues. Has opt-in triggers, shows next key information after customizable delay, allows hydra-like submodes, and more.
- [mrjones2014/legendary.nvim](https://github.com/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mrjones2014/legendary.nvim/stargazers) - Define your keymaps, commands, and autocommands as simple Lua tables, and create a legend for them at the same time (like VSCode's Command Palette), integrates with `which-key.nvim`.
- [Iron-E/nvim-cartographer](https://github.com/Iron-E/nvim-cartographer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Iron-E/nvim-cartographer?style=flat)](https://github.com/Iron-E/nvim-cartographer/stargazers) - A more convenient `:map`ping syntax for Lua environments.
- [LionC/nest.nvim](https://github.com/LionC/nest.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LionC/nest.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/LionC/nest.nvim/stargazers) - Lua utility to map keys concisely using cascading trees. Also allows binding Lua functions to keys.
- [slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim](https://github.com/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/slugbyte/unruly-worker.nvim/stargazers) - A ridiculously fun alternative keymap for the workman keyboard layout, with lots of powerful features for working with yank, marks, macros, LSP, and more. Built and configured with Lua.
- [FeiyouG/commander.nvim](https://github.com/FeiyouG/commander.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FeiyouG/commander.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/FeiyouG/commander.nvim/stargazers) - Create and manage keybindings and commands in a more organized manner and search them quickly through Telescope.

Port of Emacs Hydra. Maintained fork of anuvyklack/hydra.nvim.

- [Nexmean/caskey.nvim](https://github.com/Nexmean/caskey.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nexmean/caskey.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nexmean/caskey.nvim/stargazers) - Utility to keymappings configuration using declarative cascading trees, optionally integrates with `which-key`.
- [Wansmer/langmapper.nvim](https://github.com/Wansmer/langmapper.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Wansmer/langmapper.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Wansmer/langmapper.nvim/stargazers) - Auto translating your mappings for non-English input methods.
- [tris203/hawtkeys.nvim](https://github.com/tris203/hawtkeys.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tris203/hawtkeys.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/tris203/hawtkeys.nvim/stargazers) - Suggest new easy-to-hit keymaps and find issues with your current keymap configurations.
- [mawkler/demicolon.nvim](https://github.com/mawkler/demicolon.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mawkler/demicolon.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mawkler/demicolon.nvim/stargazers) - Use `;` and `,` keys to also repeat jumps to diagnostics (e.g. `]d`) and to [nvim-treesitter-textobjects](https://github.com/nvim-treesitter/nvim-treesitter-textobjects?tab=readme-ov-file#text-objects-move) (e.g. `]f`), in addition to repeating `t`/`T`/`f`/`F`.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.keymap](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-keymap.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-keymap.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-keymap.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` with utilities to make special key mappings: multi-step actions (with built-in steps for "smart" `<Tab>`, `<S-Tab>`, `<CR>`, `<BS>`), combos (more general version of "better escape" like behavior).
- [notomo/gesture.nvim](https://github.com/notomo/gesture.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/notomo/gesture.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/notomo/gesture.nvim/stargazers) - Mouse gesture plugin.

- [lukas-reineke/indent-blankline.nvim](https://github.com/lukas-reineke/indent-blankline.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lukas-reineke/indent-blankline.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/lukas-reineke/indent-blankline.nvim/stargazers) - IndentLine replacement in Lua with more features and Tree-sitter support.
- [LucasTavaresA/simpleIndentGuides.nvim](https://github.com/LucasTavaresA/simpleIndentGuides.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LucasTavaresA/simpleIndentGuides.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/LucasTavaresA/simpleIndentGuides.nvim/stargazers) - Indentation guides using the built-in variables.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.indentscope](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-indentscope.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-indentscope.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-indentscope.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` for visualizing and operating on indent scope. Supports customization of debounce delay, animation style, and different granularity of options for scope computing algorithm.
- [NMAC427/guess-indent.nvim](https://github.com/NMAC427/guess-indent.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NMAC427/guess-indent.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/NMAC427/guess-indent.nvim/stargazers) - Automatic indentation style detection.
- [Darazaki/indent-o-matic](https://github.com/Darazaki/indent-o-matic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Darazaki/indent-o-matic?style=flat)](https://github.com/Darazaki/indent-o-matic/stargazers) - Dumb automatic fast indentation detection written in Lua.
- [yaocccc/nvim-hlchunk](https://github.com/yaocccc/nvim-hlchunk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yaocccc/nvim-hlchunk?style=flat)](https://github.com/yaocccc/nvim-hlchunk/stargazers) - Highlight a `{}` chunk.
- [shellRaining/hlchunk.nvim](https://github.com/shellRaining/hlchunk.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shellRaining/hlchunk.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/shellRaining/hlchunk.nvim/stargazers) - A Lua implementation of `nvim-hlchunk`, contains more features, such as highlight `{}` chunk, indent line, space blank etc.
- [VidocqH/auto-indent.nvim](https://github.com/VidocqH/auto-indent.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VidocqH/auto-indent.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/VidocqH/auto-indent.nvim/stargazers) - Auto indent cursor when cursor at the first column and press `<TAB>` key like VSCode.
- [Mr-LLLLL/cool-chunk.nvim](https://github.com/Mr-LLLLL/cool-chunk.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Mr-LLLLL/cool-chunk.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Mr-LLLLL/cool-chunk.nvim/stargazers) - Simpler and faster chunking with animations.
- [gh-liu/fold_line.nvim](https://github.com/gh-liu/fold_line.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gh-liu/fold_line.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/gh-liu/fold_line.nvim/stargazers) - Lines for indicating code folding, which could achieve an effect similar to indentline by `:set fdm=indent`.

## Remote Development

- [inhesrom/remote-ssh.nvim](https://github.com/inhesrom/remote-ssh.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/inhesrom/remote-ssh.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/inhesrom/remote-ssh.nvim/stargazers) - Duplicates the basic ground level functionality of VSCode's Remote-SSH plugin, with a focus on a local editing experience to avoid remote "lag". Browse remote files, edit "remote buffers" with a full local editing experience (LSP, Tree-sitter, Telescope integration, and a file watcher).

- [mrcjkb/kickstart-nix.nvim](https://github.com/mrcjkb/kickstart-nix.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrcjkb/kickstart-nix.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mrcjkb/kickstart-nix.nvim/stargazers) - A simple [Nix flake](https://wiki.nixos.org/wiki/Flakes) template repo for Neovim derivations, with the goal of simplifying the migration from existing editor configurations.
- [drybalka/clean.nvim](https://github.com/drybalka/clean.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/drybalka/clean.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/drybalka/clean.nvim/stargazers) - Cleaning up the default key mappings and plugins and leaving only the bare essentials to build upon.
- [StratOS-Linux/StratVIM](https://github.com/StratOS-Linux/StratVIM) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/StratOS-Linux/StratVIM?style=flat)](https://github.com/StratOS-Linux/StratVIM/stargazers) - A full-fledged Neovim distribution included by default in [StratOS-Linux](https://github.com/StratOS-Linux) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/StratOS-Linux?style=flat)](https://github.com/StratOS-Linux/stargazers).
- [Shaobin-Jiang/IceNvim](https://github.com/Shaobin-Jiang/IceNvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Shaobin-Jiang/IceNvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/Shaobin-Jiang/IceNvim/stargazers) - A beautiful, powerful and customizable config that is blazingly fast.
- [ayamir/nvimdots](https://github.com/ayamir/nvimdots) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ayamir/nvimdots?style=flat)](https://github.com/ayamir/nvimdots/stargazers) - A well-configured and structured configuration with NixOS support.
- [adoyle-h/one.nvim](https://github.com/adoyle-h/one.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adoyle-h/one.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/adoyle-h/one.nvim/stargazers) - All-in-one config framework in Lua.
- [nvim-mini/MiniMax](https://github.com/nvim-mini/MiniMax) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/MiniMax?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/MiniMax/stargazers) - A collection of self-contained and extensively commented configurations which mostly use MINI tools.
- [TheItcor/MoaiVim](https://github.com/TheItcor/MoaiVim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TheItcor/MoaiVim?style=flat)](https://github.com/TheItcor/MoaiVim/stargazers) - A minimalist config that emulates a lightweight IDE.
- [plutowang/nvim.pack](https://github.com/plutowang/nvim.pack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/plutowang/nvim.pack?style=flat)](https://github.com/plutowang/nvim.pack/stargazers) - Declarative, event-driven lazy-loading configuration built purely on native Vim.pack for extreme startup performance.

## External

These tools are used externally to Neovim to enhance the experience.

### Version Manager

- [MordechaiHadad/bob](https://github.com/MordechaiHadad/bob) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MordechaiHadad/bob?style=flat)](https://github.com/MordechaiHadad/bob/stargazers) - A cross-platform, easy to use version manager.
- [NTBBloodbath/nvenv](https://github.com/NTBBloodbath/nvenv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NTBBloodbath/nvenv?style=flat)](https://github.com/NTBBloodbath/nvenv/stargazers) - A lightweight and blazingly fast version manager.
- [y3owk1n/nvs](https://github.com/y3owk1n/nvs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/y3owk1n/nvs?style=flat)](https://github.com/y3owk1n/nvs/stargazers) - Another version manager with config switcher.

### Plugin Template

- [gennaro-tedesco/boilit](https://github.com/gennaro-tedesco/boilit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gennaro-tedesco/boilit?style=flat)](https://github.com/gennaro-tedesco/boilit/stargazers) - Create boilerplate structure plugins.
- [m00qek/plugin-template.nvim](https://github.com/m00qek/plugin-template.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m00qek/plugin-template.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/m00qek/plugin-template.nvim/stargazers) - A plugin template that setups test infrastructure and GitHub Actions.
- [ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template](https://github.com/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template?style=flat)](https://github.com/ellisonleao/nvim-plugin-template/stargazers) - Another plugin template, using GitHub's template feature.
- [2KAbhishek/template.nvim](https://github.com/2KAbhishek/template.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/2KAbhishek/template.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/2KAbhishek/template.nvim/stargazers) - Opinionated template for starting plugin dev quickly.
- [jkeresman01/spring-initializr.nvim](https://github.com/jkeresman01/spring-initializr.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jkeresman01/spring-initializr.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/jkeresman01/spring-initializr.nvim/stargazers) - Scaffold Spring Boot projects with a Telescope-powered UI.
- [DrKJeff16/nvim-plugin-boilerplate](https://github.com/DrKJeff16/nvim-plugin-boilerplate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DrKJeff16/nvim-plugin-boilerplate?style=flat)](https://github.com/DrKJeff16/nvim-plugin-boilerplate/stargazers) - A documented template for new plugins generated by a script. Includes tests, CI utilities, etc.
- [chrisgrieser/nvim-pseudometa-plugin-template](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/nvim-pseudometa-plugin-template) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisgrieser/nvim-pseudometa-plugin-template?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/nvim-pseudometa-plugin-template/stargazers) - Template for new plugins.

### OS-specific

- [chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrisgrieser/alfred-neovim-utilities/stargazers) - Search plugins and online `:help` via Alfred (macOS).
- [iamironz/android-nvim-plugin](https://github.com/iamironz/android-nvim-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iamironz/android-nvim-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/iamironz/android-nvim-plugin/stargazers) - Android build, deploy, and logcat commands with Gradle integration.
- [massix/termux.nvim](https://github.com/massix/termux.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/massix/termux.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/massix/termux.nvim/stargazers) - Interact with Termux APIs, useful to gather various information about your Android phone to display in the statusline (e.g. battery level).
- [m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins](https://github.com/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins?style=flat)](https://github.com/m15a/flake-awesome-neovim-plugins/stargazers) - Nix flake that provides a collection of `awesome-neovim` plugins as Nix packages.

## UI

- [OXY2DEV/ui.nvim](https://github.com/OXY2DEV/ui.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OXY2DEV/ui.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/OXY2DEV/ui.nvim/stargazers) - A blueprint/template/guide for customizing the UI.
- [mcauley-penney/visual-whitespace.nvim](https://github.com/mcauley-penney/visual-whitespace.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mcauley-penney/visual-whitespace.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mcauley-penney/visual-whitespace.nvim/stargazers) - See whitespace characters in Visual selections, like VSCode.
- [jrop/tuis.nvim](https://github.com/jrop/tuis.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jrop/tuis.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/jrop/tuis.nvim/stargazers) - A collection of interactive TUIs which provides rich, interactive UIs to various CLIs.
- [matbme/JABS.nvim](https://github.com/matbme/JABS.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/matbme/JABS.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/matbme/JABS.nvim/stargazers) - Pretty and minimal buffer switcher window.
- [rcarriga/nvim-notify](https://github.com/rcarriga/nvim-notify) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rcarriga/nvim-notify?style=flat)](https://github.com/rcarriga/nvim-notify/stargazers) - A fancy, configurable, notification manager.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.notify](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-notify.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-notify.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-notify.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` to show one or more highlighted notifications in a single window. Provides maker of `vim.notify()` implementation and sets up automated LSP progress updates.
- [folke/noice.nvim](https://github.com/folke/noice.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/folke/noice.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/folke/noice.nvim/stargazers) - Highly experimental plugin that completely replaces the UI for messages, cmdline and the popupmenu.
- [toppair/reach.nvim](https://github.com/toppair/reach.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/toppair/reach.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/toppair/reach.nvim/stargazers) - Buffer, mark, tabpage switcher.
- [ghillb/cybu.nvim](https://github.com/ghillb/cybu.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ghillb/cybu.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/ghillb/cybu.nvim/stargazers) - Displays a notification window with context when cycling buffers.
- [CosmicNvim/cosmic-ui](https://github.com/CosmicNvim/cosmic-ui) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CosmicNvim/cosmic-ui?style=flat)](https://github.com/CosmicNvim/cosmic-ui/stargazers) - Cosmic-UI is a simple wrapper around specific Vim functionality.
- [sitiom/nvim-numbertoggle](https://github.com/sitiom/nvim-numbertoggle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sitiom/nvim-numbertoggle?style=flat)](https://github.com/sitiom/nvim-numbertoggle/stargazers) - Automatically toggle between relative and absolute line numbers.
- [nkakouros-original/numbers.nvim](https://github.com/nkakouros-original/numbers.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nkakouros-original/numbers.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/nkakouros-original/numbers.nvim/stargazers) - Toggle relativenumber whenever it makes sense.
- [cpea2506/relative-toggle.nvim](https://github.com/cpea2506/relative-toggle.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cpea2506/relative-toggle.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/cpea2506/relative-toggle.nvim/stargazers) - Toggles smoothly between number and relative numbers, supporting various number combinations, highly customizable.
- [LukasPietzschmann/telescope-tabs](https://github.com/LukasPietzschmann/telescope-tabs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LukasPietzschmann/telescope-tabs?style=flat)](https://github.com/LukasPietzschmann/telescope-tabs/stargazers) - Quickly navigate between tabs using telescope.
- [ariel-frischer/bmessages.nvim](https://github.com/ariel-frischer/bmessages.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ariel-frischer/bmessages.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/ariel-frischer/bmessages.nvim/stargazers) - Replace the default `:messages` window with a configurable, auto-updating buffer.
- [markgandolfo/lightswitch.nvim](https://github.com/markgandolfo/lightswitch.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/markgandolfo/lightswitch.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/markgandolfo/lightswitch.nvim/stargazers) - Toggle various options using the `nui.nvim` library.
- [wsdjeg/calendar.nvim](https://github.com/wsdjeg/calendar.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wsdjeg/calendar.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/wsdjeg/calendar.nvim/stargazers) - A simple floating calendar with extensions support.
- [xieyonn/spinner.nvim](https://github.com/xieyonn/spinner.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xieyonn/spinner.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/xieyonn/spinner.nvim/stargazers) - Extensible spinner framework for animated spinners in statusline, tabline, winbar, buffer, cmdline, or next to the cursor.
- [quickui.nvim](https://github.com/mjmjm0101/quickui.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mjmjm0101/quickui.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/mjmjm0101/quickui.nvim/stargazers) - Structured, keyboard-driven menus and context menus with nested navigation.
- [ln.nvim](https://github.com/markosnarinian/ln.nvim) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/markosnarinian/ln.nvim?style=flat)](https://github.com/markosnarinian/ln.nvim/stargazers) - Relative numbers on the active window, absolute everywhere else.
- [nvim-mini/mini.nvim#mini.input](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-input.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-input.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvim-mini/mini.nvim/blob/main/readmes/mini-input.md/stargazers) - Module of `mini.nvim` for getting user input with fully customizable key and view handling. Can show as floating window, statusline/tabline/winbar, virtual line/text. Provides `vim.ui.input()` implementation.

## Resource

- [Vimawesome](https://vimawesome.com/) - Showcases various plugins for Vim and has a [Neovim tag](https://vimawesome.com/?q=tag:neovim) for other Neovim-related plugins.
- [akrawchyk/awesome-vim#tools](https://github.com/akrawchyk/awesome-vim#tools) - A short list of Vim plugins and helpful guides.
- [Neovimcraft](https://neovimcraft.com) - A site dedicated to searching specific plugins and guides for building plugins in Lua.
- [Dotfyle](https://dotfyle.com) - A site for sharing and discovering configurations and plugins.
- [NeoLand](https://neoland.dev) - A beautifully crafted website for Neovim resources.
- [Weyaaron/nvim-training](https://github.com/Weyaaron/nvim-training) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Weyaaron/nvim-training?style=flat)](https://github.com/Weyaaron/nvim-training/stargazers) - A beginner-friendly tool for training your 'muscle memory' using small, repeatable tasks.
- [Nvim.app](https://nvim.app) - A modern search interface for plugins with fuzzy search, filtering, and self-service updates for plugin authors.
- [ChuYanLon/chad46](https://github.com/ChuYanLon/chad46) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChuYanLon/chad46?style=flat)](https://github.com/ChuYanLon/chad46/stargazers) - 94 themes with 44 highlight integrations, daily synced from NvChad/base46.
